## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: materials science / constitutive modeling
**Analysis**: This task models the stress-strain-temperature relationship of a material, a core problem in constitutive modeling. Stress typically increases with strain (elastic stiffness + plastic hardening) and decreases with temperature (thermal softening), with possible nonlinear coupling between these effects.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Hooke's law: sigma = c0 * epsilon (linear elastic regime)
- Temperature-dependent elasticity: sigma = c0 * epsilon * (c1 + c2 * T) (elastic modulus varying linearly with temperature)
- Power-law hardening: sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 (Hollomon-type plastic hardening)
- Ludwik hardening: sigma = c0 + c1 * epsilon**c2 (yield stress plus power-law hardening)
- Voce saturation hardening: sigma = c0 * (1 - exp(c1 * epsilon)) (exponential saturation of stress with strain)
- Swift hardening: sigma = c0 * (epsilon + c1)**c2 (shifted power-law hardening)
- Johnson-Cook strain-temperature: sigma = (c0 + c1 * epsilon**c2) * (1 + c3 * T) (hardening with linear thermal softening)
- Johnson-Cook full thermal: sigma = (c0 + c1 * epsilon**c2) * exp(c3 * T) (hardening with exponential thermal softening)
- Arrhenius thermal softening: sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 * exp(c2 * T) (power-law hardening with thermally-activated softening)
- Homologous temperature softening: sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 * (1 + c2 * T)**c3 (power-law thermal factor)
- Linear elastic with thermal expansion offset: sigma = c0 * (epsilon + c1 * T) (thermal strain contribution)
- Ramberg-Osgood inverse form: sigma = c0 * epsilon * (1 + c1 * epsilon**c2)**(-1) (nonlinear with saturation)
- Combined Voce-thermal: sigma = c0 * (1 - exp(c1 * epsilon)) * exp(c2 * T) (saturation hardening with Arrhenius softening)
- Polynomial hardening with thermal: sigma = (c0 * epsilon + c1 * epsilon**2) * (c2 + c3 * T) (quadratic hardening, linear thermal)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Strain hardening with diminishing rate → Power-law epsilon**c with 0<c<1, or saturation form (1 - exp(-c*epsilon))
- Thermal softening of flow stress → Multiplicative factor that decreases with T: exp(c*T) with c<0, or (1 - c*T**n)
- Yield stress offset (elastic-plastic transition) → Additive constant c0 representing initial yield: sigma = c0 + f(epsilon)
- Separable strain-temperature coupling → Product form sigma = f(epsilon) * g(T) when strain hardening and thermal softening are independent mechanisms
- Temperature-dependent elastic modulus → Linear or polynomial modulus: E(T) = c0 + c1*T, multiplied by strain in elastic regime
- Thermally-activated dislocation motion → Arrhenius-type exponential in temperature: exp(c0 / T) or exp(c0 * T) for flow stress
- Strain-temperature cross-coupling → The hardening exponent itself depends on temperature: epsilon**(c0 + c1*T)
- Sigmoidal stress-strain response → Logistic-like or tanh-like shape for materials with inflection in hardening curve

**Candidate 10:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + T*c2 + c3*epsilon**4 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*exp(T*c7)`

T*(c0+c2) + T*c1*epsilon. Same issue - T dependence is polynomial in epsilon, not exponential.
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 11:** `c0*epsilon**4 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*epsilon/(c4*epsilon + c5) + c6/(c4*epsilon + c5) + c7*exp(T*c8)`

T dependence is only through exp(T*c8). GT needs T*exp(-epsilon). Cannot match.

log(T) term. Cannot produce T*exp(-epsilon) or epsilon^3.

Wait - let me reconsider. The GT is c0*epsilon^3 + c2*(T-c3)*exp(-epsilon) = c0*epsilon^3 + c2*T*exp(-epsilon) - c2*c3*exp(-epsilon).

The key question throughout is: can any of these candidates produce a term that is **linear in T** and multiplied by **exp(-epsilon)**?

For Candidate 87: c2*exp(T*c3) + c4*exp(T*c5) are both exponential in T. exp(T*c3) is never equal to T for all T. Cannot match.
Candidate 87 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 88:** `T*c0*(c1 + epsilon)**c2 + c3*epsilon*exp(T*c4) + c5*epsilon**2 + c6`

T*(c1+epsilon)^c2 power function. Not T*exp(-epsilon).

Candidate 91 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 92:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**3 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4 + c5*epsilon**3`

= T*(c0 + c1*epsilon^3) + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4 + c5*epsilon^3

This has:
- T*c0: constant times T
- T*c1*epsilon^3: T times epsilon^3
- c2*exp(c3*epsilon): exponential in epsilon
- c4: constant
- c5*epsilon^3: epsilon^3

GT = 7.317*epsilon^3 + 7.950*T*exp(-epsilon) - 2283.0*exp(-epsilon)

For this to match, we need T*c1*epsilon^3 = 0 (set c1=0, since GT has no T*epsilon^3 term), and T*c0 to equal 7.950*T*exp(-epsilon). But T*c0 is T times a constant, while 7.950*T*exp(-epsilon) is T times exp(-epsilon). These are different functions of epsilon. Cannot match.
Candidate 92 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 93:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5 + c6*epsilon**c2`

T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon^c2. T dependence is T times polynomial. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 93 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 94:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2*sin(T*c3 + c4) + c5`

epsilon*exp(T*c1) and sin(T). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 94 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 95:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2 + c3*epsilon*(T + c4)**c5`

epsilon*exp(T*c1) and epsilon*(T+c4)^c5. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 95 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 96:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon*exp(T*c2) + c3*epsilon + c4`

T*c0*epsilon and epsilon*exp(T*c2). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 96 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 97:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*epsilon/(c4*epsilon + c5) + c6/(c4*epsilon + c5) + c7`

epsilon*exp(T*c1). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 97 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 98:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2 + c3*epsilon**2 + c4*epsilon`

epsilon*exp(T*c1). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 98 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 99:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*log(c4*epsilon + 1) + c5`

epsilon*exp(T*c1). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 99 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 100:** `T*c0/(T*c1 + c2) + c3*epsilon*exp(T*c4) + c5*epsilon**2 + c6 + c7/(T*c1 + c2)`

Rational T and epsilon*exp(T*c4). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 100 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 101:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*log(T*c4 + 1) + c5`

epsilon*exp(T*c1) and log(T). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 101 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 102:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon*exp(T*c2) + c3 + c4*epsilon**2`

T*c0 and epsilon*exp(T*c2). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 102 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 103:** `c0*epsilon*exp(T*c1) + c2 + c3*sin(c4*epsilon + c5)`

epsilon*exp(T*c1). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 103 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 104:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*epsilon*exp(T*c3) + c4`

T*c0*epsilon + T*c1. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 104 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 105:** `T*c0*(c1 + epsilon)**c2 + c3*epsilon*exp(T*c4) + c5`

T*(c1+epsilon)^c2. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 105 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 106:** `c0*epsilon**4 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*exp(T*c6)`

exp(T*c6) for T dependence. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 106 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 107:** `T*c0/(c1*epsilon + c2) + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*exp(T*c6) + c7/(c1*epsilon + c2)`

T/(c1*eps+c2) rational. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 107 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 108:** `T*c0*epsilon**3/(T*c1 + c2) + T*c3*exp(T*c4)/(T*c1 + c2) + c5*epsilon**3/(T*c1 + c2) + c6*exp(T*c4)/(T*c1 + c2) + c7*epsilon/(T*c1 + c2) + c8/(T*c1 + c2)`

Everything divided by (T*c1+c2). If c1=0: = T*c0/c2*eps^3 + T*c3/c2*exp(T*c4) + c5/c2*eps^3 + c6/c2*exp(T*c4) + c7/c2*eps + c8/c2. This gives T*eps^3 + T*exp(T*c4) + eps^3 + exp(T*c4) + eps + const. Has T*eps^3 but GT doesn't. Cannot match (T*exp(-epsilon) ≠ T*epsilon^3).
Candidate 108 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 109:** `T*c0/(T*c1 + c2) + c3*exp(T*c4) + c5*exp(T*c4)*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7/(T*c1 + c2)`

Rational T and exp(T*c4). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 109 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 110:** `c0*exp(T*c1) + c2*sin(T*c3 + c4) + c5*exp(T*c1)*exp(c6*epsilon)`

exp(T*c1) and sin(T). Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 110 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 111:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2 + T*c3/(c4*epsilon + c5) + c6 + c7*epsilon**c2 + c8/(c4*epsilon + c5)`

T*(c0 + c1*eps^c2 + c3/(c4*eps+c5)). T times various functions of epsilon. None of these can equal exp(-epsilon) for all epsilon.
Candidate 111 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 112:** `T*c0/(c1*epsilon + c2) + c3*epsilon**3*exp(T*c4)/(c1*epsilon + c2) + c5*epsilon**2*exp(T*c4)/(c1*epsilon + c2) + c6/(c1*epsilon + c2)`

= [T*c0 + c3*eps^3*exp(T*c4) + c5*eps^2*exp(T*c4) + c6] / (c1*eps + c2)

If c1=0: = [T*c0 + (c3*eps^3 + c5*eps^2)*exp(T*c4) + c6] / c2. This has T and exp(T*c4)*polynomial. Not T*exp(-epsilon).
Candidate 112 verdict: [NO MATCH]

---

After exhaustive analysis, the fundamental issue is that the GT contains the term **T * exp(-epsilon)**, which requires T to appear **linearly** multiplied by a function of epsilon (specifically exp(-epsilon)). None of the candidates provide this specific coupling between T and epsilon. The candidates either have:
- T multiplied by polynomial/rational functions of epsilon (not exp(-epsilon))
- exp(T*c) terms (exponential in T, not linear in T)
- epsilon*exp(T*c) terms (wrong coupling)
- No T dependence at all

No candidate can produce the required T*exp(-epsilon) term.
